# TODO.md

## Rules

- `AGENTS.md`와 루트 `README.md`를 읽은 뒤 작업 우선순위 확인은 이 파일에서 시작한다.
- 작업 중 새 task가 생기면 이 파일에 추가한다.
- 완료한 task는 체크하고, 필요한 상세 내용은 해당 workflow 문서에 기록한다.
- 이 파일은 긴 설명을 담지 않는다. 계획, 상태, 다음 행동만 관리한다.

## Next

- [ ] define terminal utility contract only after multi-case candidate-conditioned blocker validation separates wrong and correct fully covered rows without evaluation-only action inputs
- [ ] freeze terminal utility contract only after a label-free rule can connect multi-case wrong-goal, wasted-path, and map/pose behavior without evaluation-only action inputs
- [ ] define terminal utility contract only after a label-free branch produces a promotable outcome
- [ ] define terminal utility contract only after object-relation/goal-region evidence can be linked to a validated non-GT goal-validity arbitration rule
- [ ] rerun first_eval replacement detector/objective validation only after the evidence objective is category-agnostic or property-conditioned and has a fixed safety gate
- [ ] run fixed-rule category-best detector objective validation only after detector artifact association gate passes
- [ ] write policy-scale integration contract only after robust held-out detector-objective gate passes
- [ ] keep policy-scale comparison blocked until detector-objective held-out gate passes
- [ ] `postview_evidence_v2` policy-scale comparison remains blocked until a scorer diagnostic gate passes
- [ ] `postview_evidence_v2.1` relaxed_visit rescoring은 v3 scorer plan 이후 필요할 때만 재검토
- [ ] real-world deploy용 hardware-specific workflow는 실제 장비가 확정되면 작성
